b:T56993,<div id="preamble">
<div class="sectionbody">
<div class="paragraph">
<p>Mixins and Functions are a couple of the features that make SCSS stand out from plain CSS. Despite most of the many of them being now natively available, it&#8217;s still a good idea to use them to simplify the code.</p>
</div>
</div>

            </div>
        </div>
<div class="paragraph">
<p>A very common thing to do with nested elements is to have them centered horizontally and limit their width to a set value. It&#8217;s only a couple of lines of code, but I&#8217;ve found it to be a nice improvement to the overall readability. Specially knowing how long and complex CSS rules can get.</p>
</div>
</div>

                </figure>
            </div>
        </div>
<div class="paragraph">
<p>When something is not behaving as expected, and I can&#8217;t quickly figure out why, I apply a bright-colored border or outline around it. I made this mixin to quickly highlight individual elements, or entire element trees, by activating the <code>$recursive</code> option.</p>
</div>

<div class="colist arabic">
                <table>
                    <tbody>
                        <tr>
            <td>
                <i class="conum pr-2" data-value="1"></i>
                <b>❶</b>
            </td>
            <td>Based on a base font size of 16px.</td>
        </tr>
                    </tbody>
                </table>
            </div>
<div class="paragraph">
<p>Responsiveness is a must on this day and age, and it can be achieved easily using media queries. With SASS this is easier than ever before with mixins and some of the (many) features it has built-in.</p>
</div>
<div class="paragraph">
<p>This mixin is not aimed to be pixel perfect but a reference point to get started, since every project will likely need to tweak these values. By default, assumes mobile-first approach, but I find larger screen sizes easier to play around and be a bit more creative with code, so I include an option for the opposite design approach as well.</p>
</div>
</div>

<p>A perfect example of a mixin being used for something&#8230;&#8203; Oh&#8230;&#8203; Hello! I didn&#8217;t see you there. You must also be the type of person that likes to take a peek under the hood from time to time. Good for you! Here&#8217;s your egg: 🥚</p>

<p>Can&#8217;t touch this.</p>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#8AADF4;--shiki-catppuccin-light:#1E66F5;--shiki-catppuccin-dark:#8CAAEE;--shiki-everforest-dark:#E69875;--shiki-everforest-light:#F57D26;--shiki-solarized-light:#268BD2;--shiki-solarized-dark:#268BD2;--shiki-gruvbox-light:#427B58;--shiki-gruvbox-dark:#8EC07C">    &#x26;</span><span style="color:#939AB7;--shiki-catppuccin-light:#7C7F93;--shiki-catppuccin-dark:#949CBB;--shiki-everforest-dark:#859289;--shiki-everforest-light:#939F91;--shiki-solarized-light:#93A1A1;--shiki-solarized-dark:#93A1A1;--shiki-gruvbox-light:#7C6F64;--shiki-gruvbox-dark:#A89984">:</span><span style="color:#8BD5CA;--shiki-catppuccin-light:#179299;--shiki-catppuccin-dark:#81C8BE;--shiki-everforest-dark:#DBBC7F;--shiki-everforest-light:#DFA000;--shiki-solarized-light:#93A1A1;--shiki-solarized-dark:#93A1A1;--shiki-gruvbox-light:#B57614;--shiki-gruvbox-dark:#FABD2F">hover</span><span style="color:#939AB7;--shiki-catppuccin-light:#7C7F93;--shiki-catppuccin-dark:#949CBB;--shiki-everforest-dark:#859289;--shiki-everforest-light:#939F91;--shiki-solarized-light:#93A1A1;--shiki-solarized-dark:#93A1A1;--shiki-gruvbox-light:#7C6F64;--shiki-gruvbox-dark:#A89984">::</span><span style="color:#EED49F;--shiki-catppuccin-light:#DF8E1D;--shiki-catppuccin-dark:#E5C890;--shiki-everforest-dark:#DBBC7F;--shiki-everforest-light:#DFA000;--shiki-solarized-light:#93A1A1;--shiki-solarized-dark:#93A1A1;--shiki-gruvbox-light:#B57614;--shiki-gruvbox-dark:#FABD2F">before</span><span style="color:#939AB7;--shiki-catppuccin-light:#7C7F93;--shiki-catppuccin-dark:#949CBB;--shiki-everforest-dark:#D3C6AA;--shiki-everforest-light:#5C6A72;--shiki-solarized-light:#657B83;--shiki-solarized-dark:#839496;--shiki-gruvbox-light:#7C6F64;--shiki-gruvbox-dark:#A89984"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#8AADF4;--shiki-catppuccin-light:#1E66F5;--shiki-catppuccin-dark:#8CAAEE;--shiki-everforest-dark:#83C092;--shiki-everforest-light:#35A77C;--shiki-solarized-light:#859900;--shiki-solarized-dark:#859900;--shiki-gruvbox-light:#AF3A03;--shiki-gruvbox-dark:#FE8019">        opacity</span><span style="color:#8BD5CA;--shiki-catppuccin-light:#179299;--shiki-catppuccin-dark:#81C8BE;--shiki-everforest-dark:#859289;--shiki-everforest-light:#939F91;--shiki-solarized-light:#657B83;--shiki-solarized-dark:#839496;--shiki-gruvbox-light:#7C6F64;--shiki-gruvbox-dark:#A89984">:</span><span style="color:#F5A97F;--shiki-catppuccin-light:#FE640B;--shiki-catppuccin-dark:#EF9F76;--shiki-everforest-dark:#A7C080;--shiki-everforest-light:#8DA101;--shiki-solarized-light:#D33682;--shiki-solarized-dark:#D33682;--shiki-gruvbox-light:#8F3F71;--shiki-gruvbox-dark:#D3869B"> 1</span><span style="color:#939AB7;--shiki-catppuccin-light:#7C7F93;--shiki-catppuccin-dark:#949CBB;--shiki-everforest-dark:#859289;--shiki-everforest-light:#939F91;--shiki-solarized-light:#657B83;--shiki-solarized-dark:#839496;--shiki-gruvbox-light:#7C6F64;--shiki-gruvbox-dark:#A89984">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#939AB7;--shiki-catppuccin-light:#7C7F93;--shiki-catppuccin-dark:#949CBB;--shiki-everforest-dark:#D3C6AA;--shiki-everforest-light:#5C6A72;--shiki-solarized-light:#657B83;--shiki-solarized-dark:#839496;--shiki-gruvbox-light:#7C6F64;--shiki-gruvbox-dark:#A89984">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#939AB7;--shiki-catppuccin-light:#7C7F93;--shiki-catppuccin-dark:#949CBB;--shiki-everforest-dark:#D3C6AA;--shiki-everforest-light:#5C6A72;--shiki-solarized-light:#657B83;--shiki-solarized-dark:#839496;--shiki-gruvbox-light:#7C6F64;--shiki-gruvbox-dark:#A89984">}</span></span></code></pre>
                </figure>
            </div>
        </div>
<div class="paragraph">
<p>Properties like <code>box-shadow</code> don&#8217;t necessarily transition very well, as they can be expensive to compute for the browser. On the other hand, properties like <code>opacity</code> perform very well in that regard. While it&#8217;s true that this alone is unlikely to bring a website to its knees, this is a little trick can help make this effect much smoother.</p>
</div>
<div class="paragraph">
<p>Obviously, the value for the shadow itself, as well as the transition, should be adjusted as needed and possibly extracted into other variables that can be re-used throughout the code base.</p>
</div>
</div>

<div class="paragraph">
<p>This one is quite lengthy, but it&#8217;s really worth it. I don&#8217;t write tooltips every day and I forget how to do them properly, things like deciding which properties should remain open for customization, the right position, size, etc. And most importantly, how to actually use it.</p>
</div>

            <div class="admonition admonition--left tip">
                <svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
                    <use href="/sprite.svg#icon-tip" />
                </svg>
                <p>If you make this page full screen, you should see the arrow appear in this side note!</p>
            </div>
<div class="paragraph">
<p>This mixin has all of that and more, including error handling, and is as simple as this to use:</p>
</div>

                        <use href="/sprite.svg#icon-clipboard-success" />
                    </svg>
                </span>
            </button>
